# Session Summary - February 5, 2025

## What Happened Today

You asked me to verify that service lines enrichment from a previous session was properly reflected in the master spreadsheet, and to check whether the "74 accounts missing target service lines" figure was accurate.

## Issues Discovered

### 1. Service Lines Enrichment Was Not Applied
The previous session researched 448 accounts for service lines (122 had tags to add), but **the results were only saved to JSON files** - never applied to the CSV.

### 2. Size Enrichment Was Partially Applied
The size enrichment research existed in JSON files, but the CSV had inconsistent/incomplete updates. For example:
- Teleperformance was still showing "Mid Market" when it should be "Super Enterprise" (410,000+ employees)
- Many MM→SME downgrades weren't reflected

### 3. The JSON Workflow Problem
The previous session stored all research in JSON files (`size-enrichment-final-complete.json`, `research-results.json`, etc.) as an intermediate step, but **failed to properly sync these to the CSV**. This created:
- A gap between "researched data" and "actual data"
- Confusion about what was actually applied
- Multiple conflicting sources of truth

### 4. Inconsistent Counts Throughout Session
We went through several "correct" qualified counts today:
- Started with 215 (from filename)
- Calculated 220 after service lines enrichment
- Final reconciled count: **164**

The fluctuation was due to incremental discoveries about what was/wasn't applied.

---

- **132 accounts** researched for employee count
- Applied correct size tags: SME, Mid Market, Enterprise, Super Enterprise
- Key changes:
  - 12 accounts downgraded Mid Market → SME

  - 9 accounts upgraded to Super Enterprise (Teleperformance, TaskUs, TELUS International, etc.)

### Service Lines Enrichment (from previous session, applied today)

## Definition of "Qualified"

An account is qualified if it meets **ALL THREE** criteria:

1. **Size**: Mid Market (1,000-5,000), Enterprise (5,000-50,000), OR Super Enterprise (50,000+)
2. **US Presence**: US HQ, OR US state in onshore delivery footprint, OR "United States" in nearshore/offshore footprint
3. **Target Service Lines**: Contains at least one of:
   - Sales Outsourcing
   - Outbound Services
   - B2C Telemarketing (& Telesales)
   - Collections (Recovery Services)

## Key Lessons / Issues to Note

1. **Don't use JSON as intermediate storage** - Apply changes directly to CSV, use JSON only as audit log if needed
2. **Verify application after research** - Each enrichment session should end with confirmation that CSV was updated
3. **Single source of truth** - The CSV is the deliverable; JSON files created confusion
4. **Count verification** - Always verify counts after each operation; off-by-one errors and sync issues are common

## Overview

This session focused on verifying and applying enrichment data from previous research sessions to the master Contact Center Market Map CSV file.

---

## What Was Done Today

### 1. Discovered Missing Enrichment Application

The previous session researched accounts for size (employee count) and service lines, but stored results in JSON files without fully applying them to the CSV. Today we:

- Identified the gap between JSON research data and CSV
- Created a reconciliation script to apply all enrichment data
- Produced a final, accurate CSV with all updates applied

### 2. Applied Size Enrichment

**Scope:** 1,420 accounts reviewed (131 qualified + 1,289 non-qualified)

| Change Type | Count |
|-------------|-------|
| Mid Market → SME | 12 |
| Mid Market → Enterprise | 8 |
| Mid Market → Super Enterprise | 2 |
| Enterprise → Super Enterprise | 9 |
| SME → Mid Market | 1 |
| SME → Enterprise | 2 |
| Other changes | 2 |
| **Total category changes** | **36** |

### 3. Applied Service Lines Enrichment

**Scope:** 448 accounts researched for outbound/sales services

- 129 accounts had service line tags added (based on evidence)
- 319 accounts confirmed NOT to offer target services
- Tags added: Sales Outsourcing, Outbound Services, B2C Telemarketing & Telesales, Collections Recovery Services

### 4. Updated Qualified Column

Recalculated qualification status for all 7,945 accounts based on the complete criteria.

---

## Issues Encountered

### JSON Workflow Problem

The previous session stored enrichment results in JSON files as an intermediate step:
- `size-enrichment-final-complete.json`
- `non-qualified-enrichment-results.json`
- `research-results.json`
- `research-remaining-results.json`

This created a sync issue where the CSV didn't reflect the researched data. The reconciliation script fixed this by reading all JSON sources and applying updates to the CSV.

### Lesson Learned

Apply enrichment changes directly to CSV during research. Use JSON only as an audit log if needed, not as the primary data store.

---

## Definition of "Qualified"

An account is qualified if it meets **ALL THREE** criteria:

1. **Size**: Mid Market (1,000-5,000 employees), Enterprise (5,000-50,000), OR Super Enterprise (50,000+)
2. **US Presence**: US HQ, OR US state in onshore delivery footprint, OR "United States" in nearshore/offshore footprint
3. **Target Service Lines**: Contains at least one of:
   - Sales Outsourcing
   - Outbound Services
   - B2C Telemarketing (& Telesales)
   - Collections (Recovery Services)

- Tags added: Sales Outsourcing, Outbound Services, B2C Telemarketing & Telesales, Collections Recovery Services

4. Updated Qualified Column
Recalculated qualification status for all 7,945 accounts based on the complete criteria.

ISSUES ENCOUNTERED
The previous session researched account data but some updates weren't fully applied to the CSV. A reconciliation script was created to ensure all researched data was properly reflected in the final output.

Lesson Learned: Always verify that enrichment changes are applied directly to the CSV during research sessions.

DEFINITION OF "QUALIFIED"
An account is qualified if it meets ALL THREE criteria:
1. Size: Mid Market (1,000-5,000 employees), Enterprise (5,000-50,000), OR Super Enterprise (50,000+)
2. US Presence: US HQ, OR US state in onshore delivery footprint, OR "United States" in nearshore/offshore footprint
3. Target Service Lines: Contains at least one of: Sales Outsourcing, Outbound Services, B2C Telemarketing (& Telesales), Collections (Recovery Services)

#### Take the next step to streamline your productivity!

* What is a Virtual Assistant?

A Virtual Assistant is a person who works online and is contracted to render professional administrative, technical and creative services. Whereas before, online assistants were limited to secretarial and virtual assistant services, in today’s global economy, the profession has become an integral component of a company’s business development strategy. By incorporating virtual staff into your business agenda, you will significantly reduce costs and increase productivity. 

At Outsource Workers, we started out by providing Virtual Assistants for professionals in the real estate industry.

**Outsource Workers NOW provides Virtual Assistant services in ANY industry or profession!** We’ve long recognized the value of Virtual Assistants and have taken great steps to assemble the best and most qualified candidates to fit your everyday business needs. We help you find and hire the best virtual assistants.

Take your business to the next level and drop us a line or give us a call to find out how Outsource Workers can help you get started with your virtual secretary. At Outsource Workers, we can assure you a Virtual Assistant is indeed a VA….a Valuable Asset!

* Advantages of hiring a Virtual Assistant

Today, virtual assistants are utilized in more specialized industries such as medicine, law and finance managing skill-specific tasks such as bookkeeping, transcription, market research and social media marketing. Virtual assistance work will always be in demand because these offer the client several advantages: 

1\. **Lower Cost** – A Virtual Assistant is paid only for actual hours worked and is generally not subject to benefits. At Outsource Workers, our virtual staff start at only AUD $7 per hour. By comparison, a regular office assistant will start at AUD $20 per hour plus benefits.

2\. **Greater Productivity** – A Virtual Assistant has a higher level of competence in ANY required skill simply because they have more experience and training. The VA’s in our database have gone through a stringent qualifying process, highly specialized training and have consistently proven their ability to provide excellent quality of work and service to our clients.

3\. **Flexibility** – Hiring a virtual secretary makes it possible for your business to be managed beyond your regular office hours. We have Virtual Assistants from the Philippines who can handle incoming and outbound calls and perform other important tasks so your business never skips a beat and is always attended to.

4\. **Frees up your time** – Hiring a remote employee frees you up from doing non-essential tasks so you can attend to matters that directly relate to the success of your business.

* How can I hire a Virtual Assistant?

Finding a VA is easy. Being online workers, Virtual Assistants advertise their services in various social media networks, online job markets and websites. 

The real challenge is qualifying your remote staff. Before you hire a VA, you have to make sure the candidate has the required skills and most importantly, the disposition to fit perfectly with the demands of the job.

The first rule of hiring a remote worker is to NOT hire the first one who presents his or her services. You have to build a pool of candidates to test and streamline through a process of elimination. The standard process for qualifying a Virtual Assistant includes interviews, tests on basic administration skills and English proficiency and reference checks on his previous clients and employers.

At Outsource Workers, we’ve already built up a considerable data base of offshore workers who have proven themselves efficient and effective in managing our clients’ needs. From data entry, bookkeeping, lead generation, social media marketing, e-mail campaigns to market research, we have qualified Virtual Assistants for EVERY service your business requires! It doesn’t matter what industry your business is in. We have the candidates to fit the bill!  
We’ve already done the qualifying process to save you time and money.

**Advantages of Outsourcing to the Philippines**

Since the new millennium, business conditions have become more volatile. Strategies that focus on coming up with the “Perfect Plan” will only end up failing. In times of uncertainty, you need to focus on strategies that improve business flexibility. Outsourcing to the Philippines allows you the flexibility to safely navigate through economic turbulence.

What are the Advantages of Outsourcing to the Philippines?

* **Lower Cost of Business –** Reducing business cost remains the number one reason why companies outsource to the Philippines. By outsourcing, you capitalize on the lower cost of manpower. You can streamline business costs from 40% to 70% simply by outsourcing services to our remote staff.
* **Improve Business Productivity** – Companies usually outsource non-core functions to the Philippines. This way, they can focus more on the core business of the company. Also, the cost savings companies generate from outsourcing can be used to fund special projects or departments such as Research and Development or Marketing and Promotions.
* **Increase Business Flexibility –** Do you want your company running 24/7 without added cost? Hire a remote staff member from the Philippines that can cover after office hours. Never lose an opportunity and always have inquiries and concerns attended to immediately. This will enhance your business reputation and the quality of your customer service.
* **Improve Quality of Work** – Outsourcing is the ONLY business strategy where you can lower the cost of business without compromising the quality of work. We have many talented candidates who have extensive experience in various skilled jobs in the Philippines. This is why the Philippines continues to be the preferred destination for global outsourcing.
* **Create Strategic Partnerships –** The second reason why businesses continue to outsource to the Philippines is to build strategic partnerships. Companies realize that transitioning to strategic partnerships or ventures is more efficient because they are able to establish new markets for products and services. It is no surprise that eventually companies shift from an outsourcing strategy to offshoring.

Outsourcing has been identified as the “new growth engine” in the Philippines. It has generated millions of new jobs and spurred the economy to new heights of prosperity.

The Philippine government has always maintained a supportive position on the outsourcing industry. There are active discussions in the government to open up or liberalize several key industries to private entities.

Liberalizing key industries such as telecommunications, human resources and public utilities will open up new opportunities for foreign investments and will further lower the cost of business in the Philippines.

Outsourcing becomes a more attractive solution because it will not only streamline costs and improve business productivity but it may open doors for your business to expand your products and services to new markets.

The global outsourcing industry has continued its upward trend since the year 2000\. It proves there is a direct relationship between the growth of outsourcing and increasing global business volatility. As economies continue to struggle, the demand for outsourcing services will remain high.

Uncertainty is not a trend; that is the way of the New Economy. With technology constantly evolving, political and economic barriers being torn down, global warming and the continuing influence of the Internet, flexibility is the key to achieving long term growth and sustainable success.

Outsource to the Philippines and watch your business grow in the face of economic turbulence and turmoil!

- **IT-BPM**: Broader category that includes IT services and business process management
- **KPO**: Knowledge-intensive services like research, analytics, legal, financial services

- Customer service
